- parametric_update: ROTATE / SCALE

## C14 Medium Diagnostic Addendum

C14 current files:

- `docs/C14_MEDIUM_SCALE_DIAGNOSTIC_TRAINING.md`: medium diagnostic status, data gate, loader dry-run, training blocker, and next action.
- `reports/c14_autonomous_pipeline_result.json`: machine-readable C14 result.
- `reports/c14_medium_dataset_manifest.json`: 80-row medium dataset manifest.
- `reports/c14_medium_data_gate.json`: C14 data validation gate.
- `reports/c14_diffsynth_loader_dryrun.json`: DiffSynth `UnifiedDataset` dry-run result.
- `_archive/deprecated_20260622/configs/c14_semantic_repair4_medium/`: local mirror of C14 training parameters.
- `scripts/c14_train_*_20.sh` and `scripts/c14_train_mixed_80.sh`: server-side C14 command mirrors.

These files are current generated documentation/report artifacts. They do not change the current action protocol: semantic_repair4 remains ADD / REMOVE / TRANSLATE / REPLACE, while ROTATE / SCALE remain parametric_update.
### `Benchmark .pdf/` and root files (1 files)
#### `Benchmark .pdf`
